&WindowsLineEndingFormatter{\n\t\tinner: inner,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Format formats an entry and normalizes line endings on Windows.\nfunc (f *WindowsLineEndingFormatter) Format(entry *logrus.Entry) ([]byte, error) {\n\tdata, err := f.inner.Format(entry)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn data, err\n\t}\n\n\t// Only normalize line endings on Windows\n\tif runtime.GOOS != \"windows\" {\n\t\treturn data,
